# Grafana Legacy Alerting to Unified Alerting Migration

## Your Task

Find all Go source files in grafana/grafana that implement both the legacy alerting engine and the unified alerting (ngalert) engine: the legacy alert rule storage, the unified alert rule storage, and the migration script that converts legacy rules to unified format.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the migration domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/grafana--26d36ec.

```json

  ],
  "symbols": [

}
```

Include only the fields relevant to this task. Your answer is evaluated against a closed-world oracle — completeness matters.

			{Name: "eval_data", Type: DB_Text, Nullable: true},

			{Name: "new_state_date", Type: DB_DateTime, Nullable: false},
			{Name: "state_changes", Type: DB_Int, Nullable: false},
			{Name: "created", Type: DB_DateTime, Nullable: false},
			{Name: "updated", Type: DB_DateTime, Nullable: false},
		},

		},

	mg.AddMigration("create alert table v1", NewAddTableMigration(alertV1))

package api

import (
	"net/http"
	"slices"
	"strings"

	"github.com/grafana/alerting/notify"
	"github.com/grafana/alerting/receivers/schema"

	"github.com/grafana/grafana/pkg/api/response"
	contextmodel "github.com/grafana/grafana/pkg/services/contexthandler/model"
)

func (hs *HTTPServer) GetAlertNotifiers() func(*contextmodel.ReqContext) response.Response {
	return func(r *contextmodel.ReqContext) response.Response {
		v2 := notify.GetSchemaForAllIntegrations()
		slices.SortFunc(v2, func(a, b schema.IntegrationTypeSchema) int {
			return strings.Compare(string(a.Type), string(b.Type))
		})
		if r.Query("version") == "2" {
			return response.JSON(http.StatusOK, v2)
		}

		type NotifierPlugin struct {
			Type        string         `json:"type"`
			TypeAlias   string         `json:"typeAlias,omitempty"`
			Name        string         `json:"name"`
			Heading     string         `json:"heading"`
			Description string         `json:"description"`
			Info        string         `json:"info"`
			Options     []schema.Field `json:"options"`
		}

		result := make([]*NotifierPlugin, 0, len(v2))
		for _, s := range v2 {
			v1, ok := s.GetVersion(schema.V1)
			if !ok {
				continue
			}
			result = append(result, &NotifierPlugin{
				Type:        string(s.Type),
				Name:        s.Name,
				Description: s.Description,
				Heading:     s.Heading,
				Info:        s.Info,
				Options:     v1.Options,
			})
		}
		return response.JSON(http.StatusOK, result)

	AlertId int64
	Err     error
}

func (e MigrationError) Error() string {
	return fmt.Sprintf("failed to migrate alert %d: %s", e.AlertId, e.Err.Error())
}

func (e *MigrationError) Unwrap() error { return e.Err }

// FixEarlyMigration fixes UA configs created before 8.2 with org_id=0 and moves some files like __default__.tmpl.
// The only use of this migration is when a user enabled ng-alerting before 8.2.
func FixEarlyMigration(mg *migrator.Migrator) {
	cloneMigTitle := fmt.Sprintf("clone %s", migTitle)
	mg.AddMigration(cloneMigTitle, &upgradeNgAlerting{})
}

// DefaultFieldMaxLength is the standard size for most user-settable string fields in Alerting. Use this for typical string fields, unless you have a special reason not to.
const DefaultFieldMaxLength = 190

// UIDMaxLength is the standard size for fields that contain UIDs.
const UIDMaxLength = 40

// AddTablesMigrations defines database migrations that affect Grafana Alerting tables.
func AddTablesMigrations(mg *migrator.Migrator) {
	// Migrations are meant to be immutable, any modifications to table structure
	// should come in the form of a new migration appended to the end of AddTablesMigrations
	// instead of modifying an existing one. This ensure that tables are modified in a consistent and correct order.
	historicalTableMigrations(mg)

	mg.AddMigration("add last_applied column to alert_configuration_history", migrator.NewAddColumnMigration(migrator.Table{Name: "alert_configuration_history"}, &migrator.Column{
		Name: "last_applied", Type: migrator.DB_Int, Nullable: false, Default: "0",
	}))
	// End of migration log, add new migrations above this line.
}

// historicalTableMigrations contains those migrations that existed prior to creating the improved messaging around migration immutability.
func historicalTableMigrations(mg *migrator.Migrator) {
	// DO NOT EDIT
	addAlertDefinitionMigrations(mg, 60)
	addAlertDefinitionVersionMigrations(mg)
	// Create alert_instance table
	alertInstanceMigration(mg)

	// Create alert_rule
	addAlertRuleMigrations(mg, 60)
	addAlertRuleVersionMigrations(mg)

	// Create Alertmanager configurations
	addAlertmanagerConfigMigrations(mg)

	// Create Admin Configuration
	addAlertAdminConfigMigrations

package ualert

import (
	"fmt"
	"strconv"
	"time"

	"github.com/grafana/grafana/pkg/util/xorm"

	"github.com/grafana/grafana/pkg/services/sqlstore/migrator"
)

// KVNamespace is a vendored migration.KVNamespace.
var KVNamespace = "ngalert.migration"

// migratedKey is a vendored migration.migratedKey.
var migratedKey = "migrated"

// MigrationServiceMigration moves the legacy alert migration status from the migration log to kvstore.
func MigrationServiceMigration(mg *migrator.Migrator) {
	mg.AddMigration("set legacy alert migration status in kvstore", &migrationLogToKVStore{})
}

type migrationLogToKVStore struct {
	migrator.MigrationBase
}

func (c migrationLogToKVStore) SQL(migrator.Dialect) string {
	return codeMigration
}

func (c migrationLogToKVStore) Exec(sess *xorm.Session, mg *migrator.Migrator) error {
	migrationRun, err := sess.Table("migration_log").Get(&migrator.MigrationLog{MigrationID: migTitle})
	if err != nil {
		mg.Logger.Error("alert migration failure: could not get migration log", "error", err)
		return err
	}

	var anyOrg int64 = 0
	now := time.Now()
	entry := kvStoreV1Entry{
		OrgID:     &anyOrg,
		Namespace: &KVNamespace,
		Key:       &migratedKey,
		Value:     strconv.FormatBool(migrationRun),
		Created:   now,
		Updated:   now,
	}
	if _, errCreate := sess.Table("kv_store").Insert(&entry); errCreate != nil {
		mg.Logger.Error("failed to insert migration status to kvstore", "err", errCreate)
		return fmt.Errorf("failed to insert migration status to kvstore: %w", errCreate)
	}
	return nil
}

// kvStoreV1Entry is a vendored kvstore.Item.
type kvStoreV1Entry struct {
	ID        int64   `xorm:"pk autoincr 'id'"`
	OrgID     *int64  `xorm:"org_id"`
	Namespace *string `xorm:"namespace"`
	Key       *string `xorm:"key"`
	Value     string  `xorm:"value"`

// AlertingStore is the database interface used by the Alertmanager service.

	GetLatestAlertmanagerConfiguration(ctx context.Context, orgID int64) (*models.AlertConfiguration, error)
	GetAllLatestAlertmanagerConfiguration(ctx context.Context) ([]*models.AlertConfiguration, error)

	GetAppliedConfigurations(ctx context.Context, orgID int64, limit int) ([]*models.HistoricAlertConfiguration, error)
	GetHistoricalConfiguration(ctx context.Context, orgID int64, id int64) (*models.HistoricAlertConfiguration, error)
}

- **Annotations:** Remove prometheus from legacy runner [#106737](https://github.com/grafana/grafana/pull/106737), [@scottlepp](https://github.com/scottlepp)
- **MetricsDrilldown:** Remove legacy Metrics Drilldown code paths [#103845](https://github.com/grafana/grafana/pull/103845), [@NWRichmond](https://github.com/NWRichmond)
- **Alerting:** Remove legacy alerting. [#83671](https://github.com/grafana/grafana/issues/83671), [@gillesdemey](https://github.com/gillesdemey)
- **Alerting:** Disable legacy alerting for ever. [#83651](https://github.com/grafana/grafana/issues/83651), [@yuri-tceretian](https://github.com/yuri-tceretian)
- **Alerting:** Remove legacy alerting. (Enterprise)
In Grafana 11 the legacy alerting reaches the end-of-life. Users cannot enable it and Grafana will refuse to start if the settings are not updated to run the new Grafana Alerting. Migration from legacy alerting is not available as well. Grafana 10.4.x is the last version that offers the migration.

package store

import (
	"encoding/json"
	"fmt"

	"github.com/grafana/grafana/pkg/infra/log"
	"github.com/grafana/grafana/pkg/util"

	"github.com/grafana/grafana/pkg/services/ngalert/models"
)

func alertRuleToModelsAlertRule(ar alertRule, l log.Logger) (models.AlertRule, error) {
	var data []models.AlertQuery
	err := json.Unmarshal([]byte(ar.Data), &data)
	if err != nil {
		return models.AlertRule{}, fmt.Errorf("failed to parse data: %w", err)
	}

	result := models.AlertRule{
		ID:                          ar.ID,
		OrgID:                       ar.OrgID,
		GUID:                        ar.GUID,
		Title:                       ar.Title,
		Condition:                   ar.Condition,
		Data:                        data,
		Updated:                     ar.Updated,
		IntervalSeconds:             ar.IntervalSeconds,
		Version:                     ar.Version,
		UID:                         ar.UID,
		NamespaceUID:                ar.NamespaceUID,
		DashboardUID:                ar.DashboardUID,
		PanelID:                     ar.PanelID,
		RuleGroupIndex:              ar.RuleGroupIndex,
		For:                         ar.For,
		KeepFiringFor:               ar.KeepFiringFor,
		IsPaused:                    ar.IsPaused,
		MissingSeriesEvalsToResolve: ar.MissingSeriesEvalsToResolve,
	}

	if ar.RuleGroup == "" {
		noGroupRuleGroup, err := models.NewNoGroupRuleGroup(ar.UID)
		if err != nil {
			return models.AlertRule{}, fmt.Errorf("failed to create no group rule group: %w", err)
		}
		result.RuleGroup = noGroupRuleGroup.String()
	} else {
		result.RuleGroup = ar.RuleGroup
	}

	if ar.UpdatedBy != nil {
		result.UpdatedBy = util.Pointer(models.UserUID(*ar.UpdatedBy))
	}

	if ar.NoDataState != "" {
		result.NoDataState, err = models.NoDataStateFromString(ar.NoDataState)
		if err != nil {
			l.
... (truncated)

# 12.2.0 (2025-09-23)

### Features and enhancements

- ** Alerting:** Add feedback buttons for the new AI helpers (Enterprise)
- **Access:** Remove plugin app access in plugin basic role seeder (Enterprise)
- **Actions:** Infinity authentication [#109493](https://github.com/grafana/grafana/pull/109493), [@adela-almasan](https://github.com/adela-almasan)
- **Alerting:** Add GMA export to the new list page [#109784](https://github.com/grafana/grafana/pull/109784), [@konrad147](https://github.com/konrad147)
- **Alerting:** Add alerting AI buttons for cloud (Enterprise)
- **Alerting:** Add contact point filter to Active Notifications page [#109775](https://github.com/grafana/grafana/pull/109775), [@alexander-akhmetov](https://github.com/alexander-akhmetov)
- **Alerting:** Add enrichment per rule extension component (Enterprise)
- **Alerting:** Add extension point link from alert rule to grafana-metricsdrilldown-app [#108566](https://github.com/grafana/grafana/pull/108566), [@bohandley](https://github.com/bohandley)
- **Alerting:** Add feature toggle and

		service:        legacySvc,
		namespacer:     namespacer,

package legacy_storage

import (
	"context"
	"encoding/json"
	"fmt"

	"github.com/grafana/grafana/pkg/services/ngalert/api/tooling/definitions"
	"github.com/grafana/grafana/pkg/services/ngalert/models"
)

type crypto interface {
	EncryptExtraConfigs(ctx context.Context, config *definitions.PostableUserConfig) error
	DecryptExtraConfigs(ctx context.Context, config *definitions.PostableUserConfig) error
}

type amConfigStore interface {
	GetLatestAlertmanagerConfiguration(ctx context.Context, orgID int64) (*models.AlertConfiguration, error)
	UpdateAlertmanagerConfiguration(ctx context.Context, cmd *models.SaveAlertmanagerConfigurationCmd) error
}

func DeserializeAlertmanagerConfig(config []byte) (*definitions.PostableUserConfig, error) {
	result := definitions.PostableUserConfig{}
	if err := json.Unmarshal(config, &result); err != nil {
		return nil, makeErrBadAlertmanagerConfiguration(err)
	}
	return &result, nil
}

func SerializeAlertmanagerConfig(config definitions.PostableUserConfig) ([]byte, error) {
	return json.Marshal(config)
}

type ConfigRevision struct {
	Config           *definitions.PostableUserConfig
	ConcurrencyToken string
	Version          string
}
type alertmanagerConfigStoreImpl struct {
	store  amConfigStore
	crypto crypto
}

func NewAlertmanagerConfigStore(store amConfigStore, crypto crypto) *alertmanagerConfigStoreImpl {
	return &alertmanagerConfigStoreImpl{store: store, crypto: crypto}
}

func (a alertmanagerConfigStoreImpl) Get(ctx context.Context, orgID int64) (*ConfigRevision, error) {
	alertManagerConfig, err := a.store.GetLatestAlertmanagerConfiguration(ctx, orgID)
	if err != nil {
		return nil, err
	}

	if alertManagerConfig == nil {
		return nil, ErrNoAlertmanagerConfiguration.Errorf("")
	}

	concurrencyToken := alertManagerConfig.Configurat

package ualert

import (
	"fmt"
	"time"

	"github.com/grafana/grafana/pkg/util/xorm"

	"github.com/grafana/grafana/pkg/services/sqlstore/migrator"
)

// typeKey is a vendored migration.typeKey.
var typeKey = "currentAlertingType"

// AlertingType is a vendored migration.store.AlertingType.
type alertingType string

const (
	Legacy          alertingType = "Legacy"
	UnifiedAlerting alertingType = "UnifiedAlerting"
)

// CreateOrgMigratedKVStoreEntries creates kv store entries for each organization if the migration has been run.
// This is needed now that we've changed the semantics of data loss when upgrading / rolling back. If a user who previously
// upgraded were to rollback and upgrade again without clean_upgrade, then since they don't have org-level migrated states
// it will attempt to upgrade their orgs as if they had never upgraded before. This will almost definitely fail with
// duplicate key errors.
//
// In addition, this changes the entry for orgId=0 to be better named as it no longer tracks whether the
// migration has been run, but rather the current alerting type of Grafana; Legacy or UnifiedAlerting. This is used to
// detect transitions between Legacy and UnifiedAlerting by comparing to the desired type in the configuration.
func CreateOrgMigratedKVStoreEntries(mg *migrator.Migrator) {
	mg.AddMigration("copy kvstore migration status to each org", &createOrgMigratedKVStoreEntries{})

	// Adds back the entry for orgId=0 if it doesn't exist. This is not strictly necessary, but
	// helps to cover some issues with createOrgMigratedKVStoreEntries if a grafana instance on UA is downgraded to before
	// the split for org-specific migrated statuses.
	mg.AddMigration("add back entry for orgid=0 migrated status", &addBackAnyOrgMigratedEntry{})
}

package legacy_storage

import (
	"encoding/base64"
	"encoding/json"
	"fmt"
	"maps"

	alertingNotify "github.com/grafana/alerting/notify"
	"github.com/grafana/alerting/receivers/schema"

	apimodels "github.com/grafana/grafana/pkg/services/ngalert/api/tooling/definitions"
	"github.com/grafana/grafana/pkg/services/ngalert/models"
)

var NameToUid = models.NameToUid

func UidToName(uid string) (string, error) {
	data, err := base64.RawURLEncoding.DecodeString(uid)
	if err != nil {
		return uid, err
	}
	return string(data), nil
}

func IntegrationToPostableGrafanaReceiver(integration *models.Integration) (*apimodels.PostableGrafanaReceiver, error) {
	postable := &apimodels.PostableGrafanaReceiver{
		UID:                   integration.UID,
		Name:                  integration.Name,
		Type:                  string(integration.Config.Type()),
		DisableResolveMessage: integration.DisableResolveMessage,
		SecureSettings:        maps.Clone(integration.SecureSettings),
	}

	// Alertmanager will fail validation with nil Settings , so ensure we always have at least an empty map.
	settings := integration.Settings
	if settings == nil {
		settings = make(map[string]any)
	}

The answer has been written to `/workspace/answer.json`. Here's a summary of my findings:

## Summary

This is **Grafana 12.x** (commit `26d36ec`). The classic dashboard-based "legacy alerting" engine was completely removed in Grafana 11. The codebase now uses the following structure:

### Unified Alerting (ngalert) Engine
- `pkg/services/ngalert/ngalert.go` — Main service entry point
- `pkg/services/ngalert/schedule/schedule.go` — Alert rule evaluation engine/scheduler

### Unified Alert Rule Storage (SQL-backed ngalert store)
- `pkg/services/ngalert/store/alert_rule.go` — CRUD for alert rules (`InsertAlertRules`, `GetAlertRulesForScheduling`, etc.)
- `pkg/services/ngalert/store/database.go` — `DBstore` struct + `AlertingStore` interface
- `pkg/services/ngalert/store/alertmanager.go` — Alertmanager config storage
- `pkg/services/ngalert/store/compat.go` — DB model ↔ domain model conversion

### Legacy Storage (SQL-backed Kubernetes API adapter)
In the current codebase, "legacy storage" refers to the SQL-backed implementations for the Kubernetes-style API server:
- `pkg/registry/apps/alerting/rules/alertrule/legacy_storage.go`
- `pkg/registry/apps/alerting/rules/recordingrule/legacy_storage.go`
- `pkg/registry/apps/alerting/notifications/receiver/legacy_storage.go` (+ routingtree, templategroup, timeinterval)
- `pkg/services/ngalert/notifier/legacy_storage/` — SQL-backed alertmanager config storage

### Migration Scripts (legacy → unified alerting)
- `pkg/services/sqlstore/migrations/alert_mig.go` — Legacy alert DB schema (dashboard-based alerting tables)
- `pkg/services/sqlstore/migrations/ualert/ualert.go` — Main migration (`upgradeNgAlerting`, `FixEarlyMigration`)
- `pkg/services/sqlstore/migrations/ualert/tables.go` — Creates all unified alerting tables
- `pkg/servi

WHERE id = ?`,\n\t\t\t\tdashboardUID,\n\t\t\t\tpanelID,\n\t\t\t\tnext.ID); err != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"failed to set dashboard_uid and panel_id for alert rule: %w\", err)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn nil\n}\n\ntype AlertConfiguration struct {\n\tID    int64 `xorm:\"pk autoincr 'id'\"`\n\tOrgID int64 `xorm:\"org_id\"`\n\n\tAlertmanagerConfiguration string\n\tConfigurationVersion      string\n\tCreatedAt                 int64 `xorm:\"created\"`\n}\n\ntype upgradeNgAlerting struct {\n\tmigrator.MigrationBase\n}\n\nvar _ migrator.CodeMigration = &upgradeNgAlerting{}\n\nfunc (u *upgradeNgAlerting) Exec(sess *xorm.Session, migrator *migrator.Migrator) error {\n\tfirstOrgId, err := u.updateAlertConfigurations(sess, migrator)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn err\n\t}\n\tu.updateAlertmanagerFiles(firstOrgId, migrator)\n\treturn nil\n}\n\nfunc (u *upgradeNgAlerting) updateAlertConfigurations(sess *xorm.Session, migrator *migrator.Migrator) (int64, error) {\n\t// if there are records with org_id == 0 then the feature flag was enabled before 8.2 that introduced org separation.\n\t// if feature is enabled in 8.2 the migration \"AddDashAlertMigration\", which is effectively different from what was run in 8.1.x and earlier versions,\n\t// will handle organizations correctly, and, therefore, nothing needs to be fixed\n\tcount, err := sess.Table(&AlertConfiguration{}).Where(\"org_id = 0\").Count()\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn 0, fmt.Errorf(\"failed to query table alert_configuration: %w\", err)\n\t}\n\tif count == 0 {\n\t\treturn 0, nil // NOTHING TO DO\n\t}\n\n\torgs := make([]int64, 0)\n\t// get all org IDs sorted in ascending order\n\tif err = sess.Table(\"org\").OrderBy(\"id\").Cols(\"id\").Find(&orgs); err != nil {\n\t\treturn 0, fmt.Errorf(\"failed to query table org: %w\", err)\n\t}\n\tif len(orgs) == 0 { // should not really happen\n\t\tmigrator.Logger.Info(\"No organizations are found. Nothing to migrate\")\n\t\treturn 0, nil\n\t}\n\n\tfirstOrg := orgs[0]\n\n\t// assigning all configurations to the first org because 0 does not usually point to any\n\tmigrator.Logger.Info(\"Assigning all existing records from alert_configuration to the first organization\", \"org\", firstOrg)\n\t_, err = sess.Cols(\"org_id\").Where(\"org_id = 0\").Update(&AlertConfiguration{OrgID: firstOrg})\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn 0, fmt.Errorf(\"failed to update org_id for all rows in the table alert_configuration: %w\", err)\n\t}\n\n\t// if there is a single organization it is safe to assume that all configurations belong to it.\n\tif len(orgs) == 1 {\n\t\treturn firstOrg, nil\n\t}\n\t// if there are many organizations we cannot safely assume what organization an alert_configuration belongs to.\n\t// Therefore, we apply the default configuration to all organizations. The previous version could be restored if needed.\n\tmigrator.Logger.Warn(\"Detected many organizations. The current alertmanager configuration will be replaced by the default one\")\n\tconfigs := make([]*AlertConfiguration, 0, len(orgs))\n\tfor _, org := range orgs {\n\t\tconfigs = append(configs, &AlertConfiguration{\n\t\t\tAlertmanagerConfiguration: migrator.Cfg.UnifiedAlerting.DefaultConfiguration,\n\t\t\t// Since we are migration for a snapshot of the code, it is always going to migrate to\n\t\t\t// the v1 config.\n\t\t\tConfigurationVersion: \"v1\",\n\t\t\tOrgID:                org,\n\t\t})\n\t}\n\n\t_, err = sess.InsertMulti(configs)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn 0, fmt.Errorf(\"failed to add default alertmanager configurations to every organization: %w\", err)\n\t}\n\treturn 0, nil\n}\n\n// updateAlertmanagerFiles scans the existing alerting directory '<data_dir>/alerting' for known files.\n// If argument 'orgId' is not 0 updateAlertmanagerFiles moves all known files to the directory <data_dir>/alerting/<orgId>.\n// Otherwise, it deletes those files.\n// pre-8.2 version put all configuration files into the root of alerting directory. Since 8.2 configuration files are put in organization specific directory\nfunc (u *upgradeNgAlerting) updateAlertmanagerFiles(orgId int64, migrator *migrator.Migrator) {\n\tknownFiles := map[string]any{\"__default__.tmpl\": nil, \"silences\": nil, \"notifications\": nil}\n\talertingDir := filepath.Join(migrator.Cfg.DataPath, \"alerting\")\n\n\t// do not fail if something goes wrong because these files are not used anymore. the worst that can happen is that we leave some leftovers behind\n\tdeleteFile := func(fileName string) {\n\t\tpath := filepath.Join(alertingDir, fileName)\n\t\tmigrator.Logger.Info(\"Deleting alerting configuration file\", \"file\", fileName)\n\t\terr := os.Remove(path)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\tmigrator.Logger.Warn(\"Failed to delete file\", \"file\", path, \"error\", err)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tmoveFile := func(fileName string) {\n\t\talertingOrgDir := filepath.Join(alertingDir, strconv.FormatInt(orgId, 10))\n\t\tif err := os.MkdirAll(alertingOrgDir, 0750); err != nil {\n\t\t\tmigrator.Logger.Error(\"Failed to create alerting directory for organization. Skip moving the file and delete it instead\", \"target_dir\", alertingOrgDir, \"org_id\", orgId, \"error\", err, \"file\", fileName)\n\t\t\tdeleteFile(fileName)\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\t\terr := os.Rename(filepath.Join(alertingDir, fileName), filepath.Join(alertingOrgDir, fileName))\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\tmigrator.Logger.Error(\"Failed to move alertmanager configuration file to organization.\", \"source_dir\", alertingDir, \"target_dir\", alertingOrgDir, \"org_id\", orgId, \"error\", err, \"file\", fileName)\n\t\t\tdeleteFile(fileName)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tentries, err := os.ReadDir(alertingDir)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\tif !os.IsNotExist(err) {\n\t\t\tkeys := make([]string, 0, len(knownFiles))\n\t\t\tfor key := range knownFiles {\n\t\t\t\tkeys = append(keys, key)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tmigrator.Logger.Warn(\"Failed to clean up alerting directory. There may be files that are not used anymore.\", \"path\", alertingDir, \"files_to_delete\", keys, \"error\", err)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tfor _, entry := range entries {\n\t\t_, known := knownFiles[entry.Name()]\n\t\tif known {\n\t\t\tif orgId == 0 {\n\t\t\t\tdeleteFile(entry.Name())\n\t\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t\tmoveFile(entry.Name())\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n}\n\nfunc (u *upgradeNgAlerting) SQL(migrator.Dialect) string {\n\treturn codeMigration\n}"
}

`pkg/services/ngalert/schedule/schedule.go`: The alert rule evaluation scheduler/engine that runs alert rules on a schedule.\\n\\n2. **Unified alert rule storage (SQL-based ngalert store)** \u2013 the primary SQL-backed store for unified alerting rules:\\n   - `pkg/services/ngalert/store/alert_rule.go`: Implements `InsertAlertRules`, `GetAlertRulesForScheduling`, `ListAlertRules`, `DeleteAlertRulesByUID`, and other CRUD operations on the `alert_rule` table.\\n   - `pkg/services/ngalert/store/database.go`: Defines `DBstore` struct and `AlertingStore` interface for alertmanager config storage.\\n   - `pkg/services/ngalert/store/alertmanager.go`: Implements alertmanager configuration storage (save/get/update alertmanager configs).\\n   - `pkg/services/ngalert/store/compat.go`: Conversion functions between the internal `alertRule` DB model and the `models.AlertRule` domain model (`alertRuleToModelsAlertRule`, `alertRuleFromModelsAlertRule`).\\n   - `pkg/services/ngalert/store/instance_database.go`: Stores alert instance state.\\n   - `pkg/services/ngalert/store/models.go`: Internal DB model structs for alert rules and instances.\\n\\n3. **Legacy storage (SQL-backed adapter for Kubernetes-style API)** \u2013 in the current codebase, 'legacy storage' refers to the SQL-backed implementations used by the Grafana Kubernetes API server as opposed to a future etcd-backed unified storage:\\n   - `pkg/registry/apps/alerting/rules/alertrule/legacy_storage.go`: SQL-backed storage for alerting rules exposed via the K8s API.\\n   - `pkg/registry/apps/alerting/rules/alertrule/storage.go`: Factory that creates the `legacyStorage` instance.\\n   - `pkg/registry/apps/alerting/rules/recordingrule/legacy_storage.go`: SQL-backed storage for recording rules via K8s API.\\n   - `pkg/registry/apps/alerting/rules/recordingrule/storage.go`: Factory for recording rule legacy storage.\\n   - `pkg/registry/apps/alerting/notifications/receiver/legacy_storage.go`: SQL-backed storage for notification receivers via K8s API.\\n   - `pkg/registry/apps/alerting/notifications/routingtree/legacy_storage.go`: SQL-backed storage for routing tree via K8s API.\\n   - `pkg/registry/apps/alerting/notifications/templategroup/legacy_storage.go`: SQL-backed storage for template groups via K8s API.\\n   - `pkg/registry/apps/alerting/notifications/timeinterval/legacy_storage.go`: SQL-backed storage for time intervals via K8s API.\\n   - `pkg/services/ngalert/notifier/legacy_storage/config.go`: Alertmanager config store backed by SQL (`alertmanagerConfigStoreImpl`).\\n   - `pkg/services/ngalert/notifier/legacy_storage/persist.go`: Defines `AMConfigStore` interface for alertmanager config access.\\n   - `pkg/services/ngalert/notifier/legacy_storage/receivers.go`: Receiver data access via SQL.\\n   - `pkg/services/ngalert/notifier/legacy_storage/compat.go`: Compatibility/conversion functions between internal models and API models.\\n   - `pkg/services/ngalert/notifier/legacy_storage/errors.go`: Error types for the legacy storage.\\n\\n4. **Migration scripts** \u2013 convert legacy (dashboard-based) alerting to unified alerting:\\n   - `pkg/services/sqlstore/migrations/alert_mig.go`: Defines the original legacy alerting SQL schema (tables: `alert`, `alert_rule_tag`, `alert_notification`, `alert_notification_state`).\\n   - `pkg/services/sqlstore/migrations/ualert/ualert.go`: Main migration logic (`upgradeNgAlerting`) that moves pre-8.2 alertmanager configs to per-org directories, and `FixEarlyMigration` / `updateDashboardUIDPanelIDMigration` functions for migrating dashboard alert annotation data into unified alerting.\\n   - `pkg/services/sqlstore/migrations/ualert/tables.go`: Creates all unified alerting SQL tables (`alert_definition`, `alert_rule`, `alert_rule_version`, `alert_instance`, `alert_configuration`, etc.).\\n   - `pkg/services/sqlstore/migrations/ualert/migration_service_migration.go`: Moves the legacy alerting migration status from the migration log table to the kvstore (`MigrationServiceMigration`).\\n   - `pkg/services/sqlstore/migrations/ualert/org_upgrade_state_mig.go`: Manages org-level upgrade state between Legacy and UnifiedAlerting modes (`CreateOrgMigratedKVStoreEntries`).\\n   - `pkg/services/sqlstore/migrations/ualert/alert_rule_state_table.go`: Adds the alert_rule_state table as part of the migration.\\n   - `pkg/services/sqlstore/migrations/ualert/rule_group_index_migration.go`: Adds rule_group_index column to alert rules.\\n   - `pkg/services/sqlstore/migrations/ualert/created_folders_mig.go`: Migration for tracking folders created during legacy alerting migration.\\n\\nNote: In Grafana 11+, the classic (dashboard panel-based) legacy alerting engine was completely removed. The 'legacy' terminology in the current codebase refers to the SQL-backed adapter layer for the Kubernetes-style API server (as opposed to future etcd-based unified storage), while ngalert IS the unified alerting engine.\"\n}\n",
